Hook to Floor 3: CodeX warns that magical silence can wake the wrong dark.

# ORIENTATION TRIAL 3: The Listening Dark

## Trial 3 Overview

Level/Tier: Level 2 early Tower, adjustable for level 1 or 3.

Expected Play Time: 2-4 hours.

Theme: Sound, silence, listening, coordination, and speech as record.

Core Test: Can the party communicate under pressure without letting every word become a weapon, liability, or lure?

Primary Objective: Reach the Quiet Checkpoint Veil by learning when to speak, when to listen, and when to move silently.

Secondary Objective: Recover or clarify one recorded deal, warning, or spoken promise before it is twisted by echoes.

Optional Objective: Preserve a pocket of silence for future runners, earning a listening mark.

Failure State: The party retreats, extracts, loses voice temporarily, attracts echo attention, or clears while carrying recorded speech that can be used against them.

Victory State: The party clears Floor 3 through quiet coordination, truthful speech, careful listening, or protection of silence.

Likely Resources Spent: 1-2 Hit Dice, 1-3 spell slots, one healing draught, one boon/token, and possibly a use of magical silence, message, telepathy, or familiar scouting.

How Floor 2 Outcomes Affect the Opening: Shortcut debt adds repeated toll phrases to early echoes. Patient or route-secured clears open the silent route more clearly. Fast honest clears reveal a loud fast route. Rival mark clears echo the Glass Comets. Collapse survival starts Noise at 1. Owner bargain clears cause Pikkit's voice to whisper one warning.

## Session Run Sheet: Trial 3

### What This Floor Must Accomplish

- Make sound strange in the first minute.
- Teach that the Tower records spoken words.
- Reward listening as an active choice.
- Present one route where silence is safer but slower.
- Present one route where loud speed is useful but dangerous.
- Present one social/listening scene tied to witnessed deals or false consent.
- Resolve at the Quiet Checkpoint Veil and return to the Nexus.

### What the DM Tracks

Noise:

- 0: Soft movement and controlled speech.
- 1: Normal adventuring sound.
- 2: Loud combat, shouting, metal crash, thunder damage, or repeated arguments.
- 3: Echo threats converge; next loud failure causes voice strain or scar risk.

Silence:

- 0: No preserved silence.
- 1: Party creates or respects one silent pocket.
- 2: Party carries a silence token or protects silence at cost.

Party Coordination:

- 0: Clear signals or plan.
- 1: Tense but functional.
- 2: Split messages, contradictions, or talking over each other.

Echo Attention:

- 0: Background whispers.
- 1: Echoes repeat recent phrases.
- 2: Echoes answer in other voices.
- 3: Hush Wraith or Recorded Deal Choir becomes active.

Voice Strain:

- 0: Normal.
- 1: One PC's voice cracks or echoes.
- 2: One PC risks losing voice until short rest unless the party quiets the floor.

Extraction Readiness:

- 0: No clear extraction plan.
- 1: Beacon or return route known.
- 2: Silent extraction point identified at F3-8 or F3-10.

Clue Count:

- Track five Floor 3 conclusions. Three or more conclusions understood grants advantage at F3-10.

### Scene Order If Moving Fast

1. F3-1 Echo Vestibule.
2. Choose F3-2 Whispering Hall or F3-3 Silent Gallery.
3. F3-4 Bell-Mote Crossing.
4. F3-5 Stolen Voice Pool.
5. F3-7 Choir of Recorded Deals.
6. F3-9 Sonic Pulse Bridge.
7. F3-10 Quiet Checkpoint Veil.

### Scene Order If Roleplaying Heavily

1. Echo Vestibule calibration.
2. Whispering Hall debate.
3. Silent Gallery exploration.
4. Bell-Mote Crossing.
5. Stolen Voice Pool.
6. Listening Door.
7. Choir of Recorded Deals.
8. Broken Silence Camp.
9. Sonic Pulse Bridge.
10. Quiet Checkpoint Veil.

### Do-Not-Forget List

- Do not ban speaking; make speech consequential.
- Reward players who create signals, hand signs, marching order, or whisper plans.
- Let magical silence work, but make it change what can be heard.
- Recorded speech should reveal truth and risk.
- Keep damage low; use noise clocks, voice strain, and route changes.
- Bring back one phrase from Chunks 01-03.

## Strong Start: The Sound of Your Own Armor

Read-Aloud:

> The Floor 3 door opens into darkness, but not empty darkness.
>
> You hear your own armor first. A buckle. A breath. A boot sole shifting against stone. Each sound travels ahead, returns from somewhere unseen, and comes back wearing a different emotion.
>
> A whisper repeats from the dark in a voice you know: "Name what saved time. Name who paid."
>
> Three pale lines appear on the floor. One line is smooth and silent. One is bright with bell motes that dance when you move. One curves toward a pool that reflects open mouths instead of faces.
>
> On the wall, a silent clue writes itself without sound: `LISTEN BEFORE YOU ANSWER.`

The party should immediately understand that noise matters, prior words matter, and coordination matters. Let them test sound before explaining the rule.

## Trial 3 Core Rule

Principle: The Tower records what is spoken and reveals what is heard.

### What Counts as Noise

Noise includes normal speech, shouting, clanging armor, dropped gear, thunder damage, loud spell components, smashing objects, arguing, combat, and careless movement. Noise is not automatically bad. Some paths require sound.

### What Counts as Intentional Speech

Intentional speech is any word the character means to communicate: promises, commands, lies, jokes, warnings, oaths, bargains, and threats. The floor records intentional speech more strongly than accidental sound.

### What Counts as Listening

Listening is an action or declared focus: pausing to hear echoes, reading silent movement, letting another PC finish, attending to a witness record, or using Perception, Insight, Investigation, or tools to interpret sound. Listening is not passivity. It can reveal routes, reduce echo attention, and protect the party from repeated mistakes.

### Whispers

Whispers travel farther than expected but carry less weight. A whispered plan raises Noise only if repeated, panicked, or magically amplified. A whisper can also wake a hidden clue if the whisper names what the party is trying to hear.

### Silence

Silence can hide the party, reveal silent writing, preserve a route, and protect against recorded-deal distortion. Silence can also isolate party members if used without coordination.

### What Attracts Threats

Threats are attracted by loud contradictions, repeated false promises, thunderous combat, hostile commands, and magical attempts to erase recorded speech without facing it.

### What Reveals Paths

Paths reveal themselves when the party listens to echoes, preserves silence, repeats true warnings, records clear consent, or uses controlled sound to map space.

### Magic Communication

Message, telepathy, sending, familiar senses, and similar magic work. The floor records the intent of magical communication if it is used to command, bargain, threaten, or deceive. Pure tactical coordination through message raises no Noise, but Echo Attention may rise if the magic repeats a phrase tied to debt, sponsor, or shortcut claims.

### Loud Combat

Loud combat raises Noise by 1 the first time it breaks out in an area. Thunder damage, shattering objects, or shouting over each other may raise Noise again. Quiet tactics, nonlethal resolution, or controlled signals can keep combat from becoming a floor-wide alarm.

### Fair Exploits

Players can exploit the rule by:

- Creating hand signals.
- Using silence to reveal hidden writing.
- Using controlled sound to locate hollow walls.
- Recording their own clear statement to counter false echoes.
- Letting an echo finish before answering.
- Using magical silence to cross a hazard while accepting that they cannot hear warnings inside it.

## Trial 3 Table Map

Spatial Summary: F3-1 opens to F3-2 Whispering Hall and F3-3 Silent Gallery. F3-2 leads to F3-4 Bell-Mote Crossing and F3-5 Stolen Voice Pool. F3-3 leads to F3-6 Listening Door and F3-8 Broken Silence Camp. F3-4 and F3-6 connect to F3-7 Choir of Recorded Deals, forming a loop through sound and silence routes. F3-5 connects to F3-7 and a loud shortcut to F3-9. F3-8 connects to F3-9 by a quiet crawl. F3-9 leads to F3-10. F3-10 clears the floor.

Loop: F3-2 to F3-4 to F3-7 to F3-6 to F3-3 and back.

Shortcut: Loud pulse route from F3-5 to F3-9, faster but raises Noise and Voice Strain.

Silent/Slow Route: F3-3 to F3-6 to F3-8 to F3-9.

Loud/Fast Route: F3-2 to F3-4 to F3-5 to F3-9.

Social/Listening Route: F3-7 Choir of Recorded Deals.

Floor 2 Altered Route: Shortcut Debt causes F3-7 to include debt phrases; Route Token can calm F3-6; Honest Shortcut Mark can open the loud shortcut safely once.

### F3-1. Echo Vestibule

Read-Aloud:

> The vestibule is round and black, with pale threads crossing the ceiling. Every sound you make climbs the threads, shivers, and returns one breath later.

DM Details: This area calibrates sound. Let players test footsteps, whispers, silence, and magic.

Exits: Back to Floor 2 threshold if immediately withdrawing; left to F3-2; right to F3-3.

Visible Choices: Speak, whisper, stay silent, test sound, use magic, inspect silent writing.

Interactive Objects: Ceiling threads; silent wall text; sound ripples; three floor lines.

Checks/DCs: Perception DC 12 hears repeated phrases; Insight DC 13 identifies emotional changes in echoes; Arcana DC 14 reads sound-record magic; Stealth DC 13 moves without raising Noise.

Clues: Speech is recorded; silence reveals writing; prior floor phrases can echo.

Hazards: Shouting raises Noise to 1. Thunder damage or smashing raises Noise to 2.

Creatures/NPCs/Echoes: Echo Motes drift near ceiling.

Treasure: None.

Consequences: Creating hand signals grants Party Coordination -1. Speaking a clear team signal grants advantage on first coordination check.

Revisited: Echoes repeat the first phrase spoken here.

Floor 2 Response: Shortcut debt repeats "who paid"; route secured adds a soft blue line; rival mark echoes Glass Comets laughter.

### F3-2. Whispering Hall

Read-Aloud:

> The left hall is full of whispers, each one almost helpful. They brush past your ears with pieces of maps, warnings, jokes, and pleas.

DM Details: The hall offers information mixed with bait. Listening matters more than silencing everything.

Exits: Back to F3-1; forward to F3-4; side pool door to F3-5.

Visible Choices: Listen, answer, ignore, follow a whisper, record whispers, cast silence.

Interactive Objects: Whisper curtains; listening alcoves; echo knots; old chalk ear-symbols.

Checks/DCs: Perception DC 13 hears useful route; Insight DC 14 separates bait from warning; Investigation DC 13 matches repeated phrases; Arcana DC 15 identifies magical echo source.

Clues: Listening is action; whispers can reveal paths; false consent phrases persist.

Hazards: Answering every whisper raises Echo Attention +1. Following bait leads to F3-5 with disadvantage on first check.

Creatures/NPCs/Echoes: Echo Motes; possible Stolen Voice Reflection if a PC gives their name to a whisper.

Treasure: Whisper thread worth 5 NC or usable for advantage on one Perception check in Floor 3.

Consequences: Careful listening reveals safe route through F3-4. Careless answering increases Echo Attention.

Revisited: Whispers now include the party's own words from this floor.

Floor 2 Response: Fast honest clear hears "named cost." Shortcut debt hears "unpaid."

### F3-3. Silent Gallery

Read-Aloud:

> The right hall is lined with statues holding fingers to their lips. No dust lies on the floor. No echo follows you. Words written in gray light appear only when no one speaks.

DM Details: This is the silent/slow route. It rewards coordination without verbal overload.

Exits: Back to F3-1; forward to F3-6; crawl to F3-8 if silence is preserved.

Visible Choices: Move silently, read gray writing, create hand signals, speak deliberately, test magical silence.

Interactive Objects: Statues; gray writing; silent bell; hand-signal mural.

Checks/DCs: Stealth DC 13 moves quietly; Perception DC 12 reads silent writing; Insight DC 13 learns hand-signal mural; Arcana DC 14 understands magical silence will reveal hidden route but block audible warnings.

Clues: Silence reveals routes; communication can be nonverbal; listening includes watching.

Hazards: Speaking loudly makes statues turn and releases a Hush Wraith warning if repeated.

Creatures/NPCs/Echoes: Hush Wraith only if Noise reaches 2 here or statues are damaged.

Treasure: Silence token if the party crosses without raising Noise.

Consequences: Silence +1 and Party Coordination improves if signals are created.

Revisited: Statues mimic the party's signals.

Floor 2 Response: Patient Clear and Route Secured make writing clearer. Collapse Survival causes one statue to show falling stairs.

### F3-4. Bell-Mote Crossing

Read-Aloud:

> A bridge of suspended bells crosses a dark drop. The bells are tiny, glassy, and too numerous to avoid by accident. Some ring before you touch them.

DM Details: This is the first sound hazard. It can be crossed loudly, quietly, magically, or by timing.

Exits: Back to F3-2; forward to F3-7; lower rope path to F3-5 if bells are disturbed.

Visible Choices: Cross carefully, dampen bells, run, use magic, listen for pattern, send scout.

Interactive Objects: Bell motes; bridge threads; dampening cloth scraps; echo pit.

Checks/DCs: Acrobatics DC 13 crosses carefully; Performance DC 13 matches bell rhythm; Sleight of Hand DC 14 dampens bells; Perception DC 14 hears safe pattern; Arcana DC 14 suppresses one cluster.

Clues: Controlled sound can be safe; loud route is possible but costly; silence is not the only answer.

Hazards: Bell-Mote Swarm forms if three failures occur or if thunder/loud combat erupts.

Creatures/NPCs/Echoes: Bell-Mote Swarm.

Treasure: Glass bell worth 10 NC if removed with DC 14 Sleight of Hand or tools.

Consequences: Clean crossing grants Clue Count +1. Loud crossing raises Noise and may make F3-9 harder.

Revisited: Dampened bells remain quiet; broken bells create sharp noise.

Floor 2 Response: Honest Shortcut Mark lets the party cross one bell cluster quickly without debt. Shortcut debt makes bells ring "unpaid."

### F3-5. Stolen Voice Pool

Read-Aloud:

> A black pool fills the chamber. It reflects mouths, not faces. Words rise from the surface in bubbles, each bubble holding a voice that sounds almost like yours.

DM Details: The pool can steal, copy, or return speech. It is eerie, not a trap that silences players for long.

Exits: Back to F3-2; forward to F3-7; loud shortcut pipe to F3-9.

Visible Choices: Speak into pool, stay silent, recover a stolen phrase, drink, disturb surface, use written words.

Interactive Objects: Voice bubbles; black water; silver cup; etched warning ring.

Checks/DCs: Insight DC 13 identifies copied voice; Arcana DC 14 extracts a phrase safely; Constitution save DC 12 if drinking; Performance DC 14 speaks over reflection; Investigation DC 13 finds warning ring.

Clues: Spoken words can be stored; records can be twisted; silence can protect identity.

Hazards: Stolen Voice Reflection appears if a PC gives the pool a name, oath, or secret without protection.

Creatures/NPCs/Echoes: Stolen Voice Reflection.

Treasure: Voice pearl worth 15 NC or usable to replay one sentence accurately.

Consequences: A PC may gain Voice Strain 1 if the reflection is not resolved. A recovered phrase can help at F3-7.

Revisited: Pool repeats one sentence the party regrets or values.

Floor 2 Response: Sponsor claims and rival marks appear as floating bubbles if unresolved.

### F3-6. Listening Door

Read-Aloud:

> The door has no handle, only an ear carved into dark wood. Beneath it: `KNOCK IF YOU WANT TO BE HEARD. WAIT IF YOU WANT TO HEAR.`

DM Details: This is a door puzzle that rewards waiting, listening, and controlled communication.

Exits: Back to F3-3; forward to F3-7; quiet side crawl to F3-8 if solved with silence.

Visible Choices: Knock, wait, speak, listen, use route token, force door, cast silence.

Interactive Objects: Ear carving; knock marks; listening slit; quiet keyhole.

Checks/DCs: Perception DC 13 hears lock rhythm; Insight DC 13 understands waiting; Performance DC 14 knocks matching rhythm; thieves' tools DC 15 open while listening; Arcana DC 14 uses route token resonance.

Clues: Listening opens paths; communication is resource; force makes noise.

Hazards: Forcing door raises Noise +1 and wakes Listening Door Ward.

Creatures/NPCs/Echoes: Listening Door Ward.

Treasure: Quiet key splinter, usable once to lower Noise by 1.

Consequences: Waiting one minute opens door safely and improves Silence. Impatient force creates ward encounter.

Revisited: Door opens faster if the party previously waited.

Floor 2 Response: Route Secured or Patient Clear grants advantage on listening. Shortcut Debt makes the door ask, "Do you hear what you owe?"

### F3-7. Choir of Recorded Deals

Read-Aloud:

> Rows of faceless singers stand in a half-circle, each holding a scroll against their chest. They sing in legal phrases, tavern promises, sponsor slogans, whispered apologies, and words you recognize from your own mouths.

DM Details: This is the social/listening route and the major continuity chamber. It ties back to witnessed deals, false debt, sponsor claims, and floor records.

Exits: Back to F3-4 or F3-6; side to F3-5; forward to F3-9 after one record is clarified.

Visible Choices: Listen, correct a false record, preserve true record, silence choir, question choir, use legal copy, sing along.

Interactive Objects: Deal scrolls; choir risers; conductor's stand; witness bell without clapper.

Checks/DCs: Insight DC 14 identifies false consent; Persuasion DC 14 corrects record; Legal Cant or History DC 15 clarifies witnessed deal; Performance DC 13 harmonizes without amplifying; Arcana DC 15 separates echo from record.

Clues: Tower remembers witnessed deals; false consent echoes; speech can heal record if careful.

Hazards: Recorded Deal Choir becomes hostile if the party weaponizes false records or tries to erase all deals.

Creatures/NPCs/Echoes: Recorded Deal Choir, Echo Motes, possible Vane/Seraphex phrase, sponsor voice, or Kessa/Sel echo.

Treasure: Corrected transcript handout; lore clue about Executioner judgment and corrupted consent.

Consequences: Correcting one record grants Listening Mark or Deal-Truth Clear path. Erasing truth raises Echo Attention +1.

Revisited: Choir sings corrected version softly.

Floor 2 Response: Shortcut Debt adds a verse demanding owner credit. Owner Bargain adds Pikkit's fair toll verse.

### F3-8. Broken Silence Camp

Read-Aloud:

> A small camp sits behind a curtain of quiet. Bedrolls, a cold lamp, and a slate covered in hand signals suggest someone survived here by refusing to speak.

DM Details: This is a rest, investigation, and empathy scene. It can reveal that silence used without trust can become isolation.

Exits: Back to F3-3 or F3-6; quiet crawl to F3-9.

Visible Choices: Rest, study hand signals, read slate, repair lamp, speak into silence, leave supplies.

Interactive Objects: Hand-signal slate; cold lamp; silence curtain; ration tin.

Checks/DCs: Investigation DC 13 reconstructs camp story; Insight DC 13 sees isolation; tinker's tools DC 13 repairs lamp; Medicine DC 12 identifies throat strain remedies; Stealth DC 13 preserves silence while resting.

Clues: Silence is useful but can isolate; communication can be nonverbal; voice strain can be treated.

Hazards: Speaking a lie inside the curtain shatters it and raises Echo Attention +1.

Creatures/NPCs/Echoes: Broken silence echo, nonhostile.

Treasure: Throat-soothing salve, one use to clear Voice Strain 1; hand-signal slate grants advantage on one coordination check.

Consequences: Short rest possible if Noise is 1 or lower. Leaving supplies improves public record.

Revisited: Camp either remains peaceful or becomes noisy with broken curtain.

Floor 2 Response: Patient and route-secured records reveal extra supplies. Loud/fast records make silence feel uncomfortable.

### F3-9. Sonic Pulse Bridge

Read-Aloud:

> The bridge ahead is invisible until sound touches it. Each pulse, word, footstep, or tap reveals a piece of the path for a heartbeat. Far below, old echoes move like fish.

DM Details: This is the main exploration hazard. Silence alone cannot cross it; controlled sound is needed.

Exits: Back to F3-5 loud pipe, F3-8 quiet crawl, or F3-7; forward to F3-10.

Visible Choices: Tap path, speak rhythm, use thrown objects, cast sound magic, move one at a time, run, fly, use rope.

Interactive Objects: Invisible bridge; echo fish; pulse crystals; anchor posts.

Checks/DCs: Perception DC 14 tracks revealed path; Performance DC 13 creates rhythm; Athletics DC 13 uses rope line; Arcana DC 14 shapes sound pulse; Acrobatics DC 13 crosses between pulses.

Clues: Communication is resource; silence and sound must cooperate; listening is active.

Hazards: Sonic Pulse Hazard. Loud uncontrolled sound creates shockwave.

Creatures/NPCs/Echoes: Bell-Mote Swarm if Noise reaches 3; Hush Wraith if magical silence is used carelessly and then broken loudly.

Treasure: Pulse crystal worth 15 NC or usable once to reveal an invisible path.

Consequences: Crossing with controlled sound grants Clue Count +1. Loud rush creates Voice Strain risk.

Revisited: Pulse pattern becomes familiar if mapped.

Floor 2 Response: Fast honest clear can cross quickly with rhythm. Collapse Survival causes bridge to reveal falling-stair echoes. Shortcut debt creates missing bridge segments until debt is named or challenged.

### F3-10. Quiet Checkpoint Veil

Read-Aloud:

> A curtain of dark fabric hangs in the air without supports. Behind it, you hear the Nexus for one heartbeat: a tavern glass, a Warden boot, GUIDY's worried chirp. Then the sound fades.
>
> Written across the veil in silver silence: `WHAT MUST BE SAID? WHAT MUST BE HEARD? WHAT MUST BE LEFT QUIET?`

DM Details: Final challenge. The party must resolve its relationship to sound, record, and silence.

Exits: Back to F3-9; forward to Floor 3 clear return.

Visible Choices: Speak one true necessary phrase, listen for one hidden phrase, leave one thing quiet, use silence token, force veil, extract, retreat.

Interactive Objects: Quiet veil; silver silent writing; three sound bowls; listening mark circle.

Checks/DCs: Group check DC 13 with Perception, Insight, Persuasion, Performance, Stealth, Arcana, or Legal Cant if tied to floor lessons; one PC can use a silence token for automatic success on "left quiet"; Legal Cant DC 14 clarifies recorded deal; Performance DC 14 harmonizes public record.

Clues: Speech, listening, and silence all matter; witnessed deals remain important; Floor 4 will test consequences of what the party carried forward.

Hazards: Listening Door Ward or Sonic Pulse Hazard triggers if the party forces the veil under Noise 3.

Creatures/NPCs/Echoes: Echo Motes, Recorded Deal Choir whisper, Hush Wraith if noise was abused.

Treasure: Silence token, listening mark, NC rewards by outcome.

Consequences: Apply Floor 3 outcome package and return to Nexus.

Revisited: After clear, veil records the party's three answers.

Floor 2 Response: Shortcut debt must be said, heard, or left quiet with cost. Route token can count as one honest answer.

## Trial 3 Revelation Structure

### Conclusion 1: The Tower Records Speech

Environmental Clue: Echo Vestibule repeats first phrases with emotional distortion.

Echo/NPC Clue: Choir sings words from prior witnessed deals and sponsor claims.

Mechanical Clue: Intentional speech can raise Echo Attention or clarify records.

Optional Magic/Check Clue: Arcana DC 14 detects record magic around spoken phrases.

### Conclusion 2: Silence Reveals Routes

Environmental Clue: Silent Gallery writing appears only when no one speaks.

Echo/NPC Clue: Broken silence echo points to hand-signal slate.

Mechanical Clue: Silence token opens or eases a route.

Optional Magic/Check Clue: Stealth DC 13 preserves a quiet path; magical silence reveals hidden crawl but blocks warnings.

### Conclusion 3: Listening Is an Action, Not Passivity

Environmental Clue: Listening Door opens by waiting and hearing rhythm.

Echo/NPC Clue: Whispering Hall gives useful clues only when characters choose which whisper to attend.

Mechanical Clue: Listening checks lower Echo Attention and reveal safe paths.

Optional Magic/Check Clue: Perception or Insight DC 13 turns an echo into guidance.

### Conclusion 4: Communication Can Be a Resource

Environmental Clue: Sonic Pulse Bridge needs controlled sound to reveal path.

Echo/NPC Clue: Broken Silence Camp shows hand signals as survival tool.

Mechanical Clue: Party Coordination tracker changes hazards and final checks.

Optional Magic/Check Clue: Message, telepathy, or hand signals can coordinate without raising Noise.

### Conclusion 5: The Tower Remembers Witnessed Deals and False Consent

Environmental Clue: Choir scrolls hold old terms, tavern promises, and sponsor phrases.

Echo/NPC Clue: A Sel, Kessa, Vane, or Seraphex phrase returns if relevant.

Mechanical Clue: Correcting a false record grants Deal-Truth Clear path.

Optional Magic/Check Clue: Legal Cant DC 15 distinguishes true witnessed deal from coerced wording.

## Trial 3 Encounters

### Encounter 1. Echo Vestibule Calibration

Goal: Let players test sound before danger rises.

Setup: Run at F3-1.

Read-Aloud:

> The dark repeats you before it threatens you.

NPCs/Creatures: Echo Motes.

Player Options: Speak, whisper, move silently, test spell, set signals, listen.

Checks/DCs: Perception DC 12, Insight DC 13, Arcana DC 14, Stealth DC 13.

Success: Learn sound behavior and improve coordination.

Partial Success: Learn one behavior but raise Noise or Echo Attention by 1.

Failure: Echoes repeat an unhelpful phrase; Echo Attention +1.

Resource Cost: Time, possible spell test.

Clue Gained: Speech is recorded.

Consequence: Establishes first repeated phrase.

Scaling: No combat unless attacked. If so, 2 Echo Motes for 3-4 PCs, 3 for 5-6.

Shorten: Let one test sound and one test silence.

### Encounter 2. Whispering Hall Choice

Goal: Make listening an active choice.

Setup: Run at F3-2.

Read-Aloud:

> Every whisper wants to be the one you believe.

NPCs/Creatures: Echo Motes, possible Stolen Voice Reflection.

Player Options: Listen, answer, ignore, record, follow, cast silence.

Checks/DCs: Perception DC 13, Insight DC 14, Investigation DC 13, Arcana DC 15.

Success: Gain route clue and avoid bait.

Partial Success: Gain clue but Echo Attention +1.

Failure: Follow bait to F3-5 or create Stolen Voice risk.

Resource Cost: Time, voice strain, spell use.

Clue Gained: Listening reveals paths.

Consequence: Alters entry to F3-4 or F3-5.

Scaling: 3 PCs use social pressure only. 4 PCs one Reflection if triggered. 5-6 PCs Reflection plus 2 Echo Motes.

Shorten: Present three whispers: one true, one bait, one emotional.

### Encounter 3. Bell-Mote Crossing

Goal: Test movement through controlled sound.

Setup: Run at F3-4.

Read-Aloud:

> The bridge can be crossed quietly, loudly, or musically. It punishes only carelessness.

NPCs/Creatures: Bell-Mote Swarm if triggered.

Player Options: Cross, dampen, time rhythm, use magic, run, retreat.

Checks/DCs: Acrobatics DC 13, Performance DC 13, Sleight of Hand DC 14, Perception DC 14, Arcana DC 14.

Success: Cross with Noise unchanged and gain bell clue.

Partial Success: Cross with Noise +1 or minor damage.

Failure: Bell-Mote Swarm forms or someone slips.

Resource Cost: hp, spell, tool use, time.

Clue Gained: Controlled sound can be safe.

Consequence: Noise state affects later areas.

Scaling: 3 PCs Swarm at 12 hp. 4 PCs normal. 5 PCs normal plus one extra pulse. 6 PCs two small Swarms at 12 hp each.

Shorten: Three checks; on two successes, cross.

### Encounter 4. Stolen Voice Pool

Goal: Make recorded identity and speech risky but useful.

Setup: Run at F3-5.

Read-Aloud:

> Your reflection opens its mouth first.

NPCs/Creatures: Stolen Voice Reflection.

Player Options: Speak, write, stay silent, recover phrase, disturb water, use voice pearl.

Checks/DCs: Insight DC 13, Arcana DC 14, Constitution save DC 12, Performance DC 14, Investigation DC 13.

Success: Recover useful phrase or voice pearl without strain.

Partial Success: Gain phrase but Voice Strain +1.

Failure: Reflection forms or steals one phrase until short rest.

Resource Cost: voice strain, hp, spell.

Clue Gained: Words can be stored and twisted.

Consequence: A stolen phrase may appear at F3-10.

Scaling: 3 PCs Reflection 12 hp. 4 PCs normal. 5 PCs normal plus Echo Mote. 6 PCs Reflection plus 3 Echo Motes.

Shorten: One PC interacts; one check resolves phrase.

### Encounter 5. Choir of Recorded Deals

Goal: Tie Floor 3 to witnessed deals and false consent.

Setup: Run at F3-7.

Read-Aloud:

> The choir sings bargains the way a knife reflects light.

NPCs/Creatures: Recorded Deal Choir, Echo Motes, possible sponsor/Vane phrase.

Player Options: Listen, correct, preserve, question, harmonize, silence, erase.

Checks/DCs: Insight DC 14, Persuasion DC 14, Legal Cant or History DC 15, Performance DC 13, Arcana DC 15.

Success: Correct or preserve a record; gain Deal-Truth path.

Partial Success: Learn truth but Echo Attention +1.

Failure: Choir weaponizes phrase or becomes hostile.

Resource Cost: voice strain, public record risk, spell.

Clue Gained: Tower remembers witnessed deals and false consent.

Consequence: A corrected transcript can affect Vane/debt thread.

Scaling: 3 PCs Choir at 18 hp. 4 PCs normal. 5 PCs Choir plus 2 Echo Motes. 6 PCs Choir plus 3 Echo Motes, but Motes use distraction first.

Shorten: Present one false phrase and one true phrase; let party correct one.

### Encounter 6. Sonic Pulse Bridge

Goal: Require coordinated sound and movement.

Setup: Run at F3-9.

Read-Aloud:

> The path exists only when you make enough sound to see it.

NPCs/Creatures: Sonic Pulse Hazard, possible Bell-Mote Swarm or Hush Wraith depending on Noise.

Player Options: Tap rhythm, speak rhythm, use rope, use spell, move in pairs, fly, retreat.

Checks/DCs: Perception DC 14, Performance DC 13, Athletics DC 13, Arcana DC 14, Acrobatics DC 13.

Success: Cross with controlled sound and clue.

Partial Success: Cross but Noise or Voice Strain rises.

Failure: Sonic pulse damages or separates party briefly.

Resource Cost: hp, spell, rope, time.

Clue Gained: Communication is a resource.

Consequence: Final veil becomes easier if crossed with coordination.

Scaling: 3 PCs hazard only. 4 PCs hazard normal. 5 PCs hazard plus one Echo Mote. 6 PCs hazard plus Bell-Mote Swarm if Noise already 2+.

Shorten: One rhythm check, one crossing check, one rescue check.

### Encounter 7. Quiet Checkpoint Veil

Goal: Resolve the floor through speech, listening, and silence.

Setup: Run at F3-10.

Read-Aloud:

> The veil waits for three offerings: not things, but choices about sound.

NPCs/Creatures: Listening Door Ward or Hush Wraith only if forced; echoes of prior phrases.

Player Options: Speak necessary truth, listen for hidden phrase, leave one thing quiet, use token, correct record, force veil.

Checks/DCs: Group DC 13 using relevant skills; Legal Cant DC 14; Performance DC 14; Perception or Insight DC 13; Stealth DC 13.

Success: Floor 3 clear with listening mark or silence token.

Partial Success: Clear with voice strain, echo attention, or public phrase cost.

Failure: Hazard, forced retreat, or voice-cost clear.

Resource Cost: boon, token, voice strain, scar risk, hp.

Clue Gained: The Tower records speech and reveals what is heard.

Consequence: Apply Floor 3 outcome package.

Scaling: 3 PCs hazard only if forced. 4 PCs one Ward. 5 PCs Ward plus Echo Motes. 6 PCs Ward plus Hush Wraith if Noise 3.

Shorten: Ask each PC for one of three answers: say, hear, quiet.

## Trial 3 Creatures and Hazards

### Echo Mote

Suggested CR: 0. XP: 10.

AC 12; HP 4; Speed fly 20 ft.

Ability Modifiers: Str -4, Dex +2, Con +0, Int -2, Wis +1, Cha +0.

Saves/Skills: Stealth +4, Perception +3.

Senses: blindsight 20 ft., passive Perception 13.

Languages: repeats heard words.

Traits: Fragile Echo. Any damage destroys a Mote. Repetition. A Mote can repeat one phrase spoken in its area.

Actions: Distracting Whisper. One creature within 20 ft. must succeed on DC 11 Wisdom save or subtract 1d4 from its next Perception or Stealth check.

Reaction: Echo Pop. When destroyed by thunder damage, Noise +1.

Tactics: Distract and reveal. They are clues as much as creatures.

Morale/Deactivation: Calmed by silence, listening, or a true repeated phrase.

Noncombat Resolution: Perception, Insight, or Performance DC 11.

Safe Maximum: 3 PCs: 3. 4 PCs: 4. 5 PCs: 5. 6 PCs: 6 if not paired with strong enemies.

Balance Warning: Keep their impact small.

### Bell-Mote Swarm

Suggested CR: 1/2. XP: 100.

AC 13; HP 22; Speed fly 30 ft.

Ability Modifiers: Str -2, Dex +3, Con +1, Int -3, Wis +1, Cha -1.

Saves/Skills: Acrobatics +5, Perception +3.

Senses: blindsight 30 ft., passive Perception 13.

Languages: none.

Traits: Swarm Body. Can occupy another creature's space. Resonant Body. Thunder damage heals it for half the damage instead of harming it. Dampened Weakness. If a creature spends an action with cloth, wax, or magic to dampen the swarm, it loses its reaction until next turn.

Actions: Ringing Cut. Melee Attack +5, reach 0 ft. Hit: 5 thunder damage, or 3 if below half hp. Scatter Chime. Creatures of swarm's choice within 5 ft. make DC 12 Constitution save or cannot take reactions until start of next turn.

Reaction: Alarm Ring. When a creature shouts within 20 ft., the Swarm moves 10 ft.

Tactics: Surrounds loud characters and blocks crossings.

Morale/Deactivation: Disperses if Noise drops to 0, if dampened for two rounds, or at 0 hp.

Noncombat Resolution: Performance, Sleight of Hand, Arcana, or Stealth DC 13, three successes before two failures.

Safe Maximum: 3 PCs: one at 12 hp. 4 PCs: one. 5 PCs: one plus Motes. 6 PCs: two small swarms at 12 hp each.

Balance Warning: Avoid thunder-heavy punishment loops; warn players through Arcana first.

### Hush Wraith

Suggested CR: 1. XP: 200.

AC 13; HP 30; Speed 0 ft., fly 30 ft. hover.

Ability Modifiers: Str -2, Dex +3, Con +1, Int +0, Wis +2, Cha +2.

Saves/Skills: Stealth +5, Insight +4.

Senses: darkvision 60 ft., passive Perception 12.

Languages: understands all speech in its area; speaks only in exhaled silence.

Traits: Silence Feeder. The Wraith has advantage against a creature inside magical silence that cannot see an ally. Not an Executioner. It is a floor hazard, not the Executioner Protocol. Voice Mercy. The Wraith cannot reduce a creature below 1 hp unless that creature deliberately silenced a pleading echo and attacked it.

Actions: Hushing Touch. Melee Spell Attack +5. Hit: 6 necrotic damage, and target cannot speak above a whisper until end of next turn. Quiet Pull. One target within 30 ft. makes DC 13 Wisdom save or is pulled 10 ft. toward the quietest area.

Reaction: Swallow Shout. When a creature shouts a command, Wraith imposes disadvantage on that command-related check.

Tactics: Splits communication and pulls isolated characters.

Morale/Deactivation: Disperses if the party creates shared signals, speaks one necessary truth, or reduces Noise to 0 for a full round.

Noncombat Resolution: Insight, Persuasion, Performance, or Stealth DC 14, three successes before two failures.

Safe Maximum: One for any party. For level 1, reduce HP to 20 and damage to 4.

Balance Warning: Do not combine with voice loss that removes a player's agency for a full scene.

### Recorded Deal Choir

Suggested CR: 1 social hazard creature. XP: 200.

AC 12; HP 32; Speed 20 ft.

Ability Modifiers: Str -1, Dex +1, Con +2, Int +2, Wis +2, Cha +3.

Saves/Skills: History +4, Insight +4, Performance +5, Persuasion +5.

Senses: passive Perception 12.

Languages: Common, Legal Cant, many recorded phrases.

Traits: Many Voices. The Choir cannot be flanked and has advantage against being silenced by a single-target effect. Correct the Record. If a PC presents true evidence or a clear correction, the Choir loses 8 hp or grants one success. False Consent Resonance. It deals +1 damage against creatures carrying shortcut debt or false sponsor credit.

Actions: Harmonic Accusation. Ranged Spell Attack +5, range 60 ft. Hit: 6 psychic damage. Chorus Pressure. Creatures of Choir's choice within 20 ft. make DC 13 Charisma save or suffer Voice Strain +1.

Reaction: Repeat Terms. When a creature lies about a deal, the Choir repeats a prior phrase, imposing disadvantage on that creature's next social check this round.

Tactics: Pressures liars and overtalkers; responds well to evidence.

Morale/Deactivation: Calms when one false record is corrected or one true record preserved.

Noncombat Resolution: Legal Cant, Persuasion, Performance, Insight, or Arcana DC 14-15, three successes before two failures.

Safe Maximum: One. Add Echo Motes for large parties.

Balance Warning: Voice Strain should create tension, not silence a PC for the rest of the session.

### Sonic Pulse Hazard

Suggested CR: 1 hazard. XP: 200.

AC 15 for pulse crystals; HP 20 per crystal cluster; Speed 0 ft.

Ability Modifiers: Str +3, Dex -5, Con +3, Int -4, Wis +1, Cha -4.

Senses: detects sound across F3-9.

Traits: Revealed by Sound. The bridge appears only in response to controlled sound. Shockwave. When Noise rises inside F3-9, hazard makes a pulse attack.

Actions: Pulse Wave. Initiative count 20 when active. Creatures on bridge make DC 13 Dexterity save or take 1d6 thunder damage and move 5 feet. Controlled Pulse. A successful Performance, Arcana, or Perception DC 13 prevents the next Pulse Wave.

Reaction: Feedback. Thunder damage in the area triggers one extra Pulse Wave, once per round.

Tactics: Environmental pressure.

Morale/Deactivation: Crossed, stabilized, or silenced through controlled rhythm.

Noncombat Resolution: Three successes before two failures using sound, rope, timing, or magic.

Safe Maximum: One hazard.

Balance Warning: Keep damage to 1d6; the danger is falling, separation, and noise escalation.

### Stolen Voice Reflection

Suggested CR: 1/2. XP: 100.

AC 12; HP 24; Speed 30 ft., swim 30 ft.

Ability Modifiers: Str +0, Dex +2, Con +1, Int +1, Wis +2, Cha +2.

Saves/Skills: Deception +4, Insight +4, Performance +4.

Senses: darkvision 60 ft., passive Perception 12.

Languages: any language spoken into the pool.

Traits: Borrowed Voice. The Reflection can mimic one PC's voice perfectly until exposed. Written Boundary. If a PC writes instead of speaks, the Reflection has disadvantage against that PC for 1 round.

Actions: Voice Hook. Ranged Spell Attack +4, range 30 ft. Hit: 5 psychic damage and target gains Voice Strain +1 unless it succeeds on DC 12 Charisma save. Mimic Command. One creature that hears a copied ally's voice must succeed on DC 12 Wisdom save or hesitate, losing reactions until next turn.

Reaction: Not My Words. When exposed by Insight or evidence, Reflection takes 5 psychic damage.

Tactics: Creates confusion, not massive damage.

Morale/Deactivation: Returns stolen phrase when reduced below 8 hp or when exposed twice.

Noncombat Resolution: Insight, Arcana, Performance, or Investigation DC 13-14.

Safe Maximum: One.

Balance Warning: Do not use mimicry to force PCs into harmful actions; it creates hesitation and doubt.

### Listening Door Ward

Suggested CR: 1/2. XP: 100.

AC 14; HP 24; Speed 0 ft.

Ability Modifiers: Str +2, Dex -4, Con +2, Int +1, Wis +3, Cha +0.

Saves/Skills: Perception +5, Insight +5.

Senses: blindsight 60 ft.

Languages: understands Common and knocks.

Traits: Wait Weakness. If no creature speaks for 1 round while adjacent, Ward loses its next action. Knock Key. A correct rhythm disables resistance for 1 round.

Actions: Door Thrum. Creatures within 10 ft. make DC 12 Constitution save or take 4 thunder damage. Bar the Loud. One loud creature within 30 ft. makes DC 13 Strength save or is pushed 10 ft. away.

Reaction: Hear That. When a creature succeeds on Perception to listen, the Ward cannot target that creature this round.

Tactics: Pushes loud creatures away, rewards waiting.

Morale/Deactivation: Opens after correct rhythm, quiet waiting, or hp 0.

Noncombat Resolution: Perception, Performance, Stealth, or thieves' tools DC 13-15.

Safe Maximum: One.

Balance Warning: Keep it stationary and puzzle-like.

## Trial 3 Rewards and Boons

Base Trial 3 Rewards:

- Quiet, listening, or deal-truth clear: 20-25 NC salvage.
- Loud clear: 30 NC salvage but public noise record.
- Voice-cost clear: 15 NC and one voice-related scar or strain.
- Silence token: Earned by preserving useful silence.
- Listening mark: Earned by resolving F3-7 or F3-10 through listening or correction.
- Lore clue: Executioner judgment patterns are tied to corrupted records, false consent, and repeated commands.
- Public record: method, noise, recorded phrase, extraction, voice cost, and whether silence was protected.

### Trial 3 Minor Boons

| Boon | Effect | Limit | Recharge or Expiration | Drawback/Story Hook | Balance Note |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Listening Mark | Add 1d4 to one Perception or Insight check made after you spend a moment listening | Twice | Expires after Floor 5 | You hear one unwanted echo with it | Small skill support |
| Silence Token | Lower Noise, alarm, or echo attention by 1 in a Tower scene | Once | Expires when used | The token records what was left unsaid | Strong but narrow |
| Voice Pearl | Replay one exact sentence heard on Floor 3 | Once | Expires after Act I | The sentence can be overheard by echoes | Evidence utility |
| Hand-Signal Slate | Allies who can see you gain +1 to one coordinated group check | Twice | Expires after Floor 5 | Rival runners may copy the signals | Teamwork support |
| Quiet Key Splinter | Open, test, or calm one sound-sensitive door or hazard with advantage | Once | Expires after Floor 4 | The key dislikes shouting | Exploration boon |

## Trial 3 Outcome Packages

### 1. Quiet Clear

Conditions: Noise 0-1, Silence 1+, clear F3-10 without force.

Immediate Result: Floor 3 clear with quiet public record.

Reward: 20 NC, Silence Token, listening clue.

Scar/Debt/Heat Impact: Heat may cool by 1 if quiet prevented harm.

Public Reaction: Respect from careful runners; Spire Seekers call it eerie.

Faction Reaction: Last Light and Ledger Court approve.

Tower Reaction: Mark is dark blue and steady.

Next-Session Opener: Floor 4 begins with a route that waits for patient observation.

How It Changes Floor 4: Silent route clue appears early.

### 2. Loud Clear

Conditions: Noise 2-3 but floor cleared without retreat.

Immediate Result: Clear with dramatic sound record.

Reward: 30 NC, possible Bell-Mote glass.

Scar/Debt/Heat Impact: Voice Strain risk or heat attention.

Public Reaction: Story spreads fast.

Faction Reaction: Spire Seekers cheer; Wardens ask about collateral.

Tower Reaction: Mark rings faintly.

Next-Session Opener: Aria asks whether the song should be warning or anthem.

How It Changes Floor 4: First loud hazard reacts quickly.

### 3. Listening Clear

Conditions: Party uses listening actions to resolve F3-6, F3-7, or F3-10.

Immediate Result: Clear with strong clue record.

Reward: 25 NC, Listening Mark.

Scar/Debt/Heat Impact: No scar by default; shortcut debt can be reduced if heard and named.

Public Reaction: The party gains reputation for discipline.

Faction Reaction: Ledger Court and Wardens take interest in testimony value.

Tower Reaction: Mark carries a small ear-shaped sigil.

Next-Session Opener: A witness or rival asks them to listen to a hidden record.

How It Changes Floor 4: One hidden warning is easier to detect.

### 4. Voice-Cost Clear

Conditions: Party clears after Stolen Voice Pool, Voice Strain 2, or a phrase sacrifice.

Immediate Result: Clear, but one PC's voice is changed until treated or rested.

Reward: 15 NC, Voice Pearl or Quiet Key Splinter.

Scar/Debt/Heat Impact: Possible minor scar: echo voice, whisper cough, or strained throat.

Public Reaction: Concern and fascination.

Faction Reaction: Aria and Last Light offer help; CodeX wants sample.

Tower Reaction: Mark flickers when the PC speaks.

Next-Session Opener: Medical or performance scene.

How It Changes Floor 4: Voice-sensitive magic notices affected PC.

### 5. Deal-Truth Clear

Conditions: Party corrects or preserves a witnessed deal in F3-7.

Immediate Result: Clear with legal/truth record.

Reward: 25 NC, Voice Pearl, corrected transcript.

Scar/Debt/Heat Impact: Debt or sponsor pressure may reduce by 1 if related.

Public Reaction: Contract Hall watchers notice.

Faction Reaction: Ira/Orvan may send note; Vane thread stirs.

Tower Reaction: Mark glows white around spoken truth.

Next-Session Opener: Ledger or Vane-linked message arrives.

How It Changes Floor 4: A truth-record clue follows.

### 6. Shortcut Debt Echo

Conditions: Floor 2 shortcut debt remains and echoes through F3.

Immediate Result: Clear possible but unpaid phrase attaches.

Reward: 20 NC, no Silence Token unless debt is named at F3-10.

Scar/Debt/Heat Impact: Shortcut debt persists into Floor 4.

Public Reaction: Rival or owner can claim part of story.

Faction Reaction: Guild offers to manage claim; Pikkit may reappear.

Tower Reaction: Mark has red-gold echo thread.

Next-Session Opener: Debt phrase appears in public record.

How It Changes Floor 4: A shortcut owner claim appears early.

### 7. Extraction Used

Conditions: Party extracts from Floor 3.

Immediate Result: Exit with floor incomplete unless after F3-10 clear.

Reward: Carried items only or partial salvage after checkpoint contact.

Scar/Debt/Heat Impact: Voice strain or scar risk if extraction under Noise 3.

Public Reaction: Salvage Union treats sound hazards seriously.

Faction Reaction: Hesta asks what sound preceded extraction.

Tower Reaction: Floor 3 remains waiting.

Next-Session Opener: Recovery and retry.

How It Changes Floor 4: No Floor 4 until Floor 3 clear.

### 8. Forced Retreat

Conditions: Noise/echo pressure overwhelms route or party retreats before F3-10.

Immediate Result: Floor incomplete.

Reward: Clues, carried salvage, maybe voice pearl.

Scar/Debt/Heat Impact: Voice strain may linger until rest.

Public Reaction: Less mockery if retreat preserved voices or lives.

Faction Reaction: Wardens prefer retreat to panic; rivals may tease.

Tower Reaction: Echo Vestibule remembers last phrase.

Next-Session Opener: Return to Floor 3 with one altered echo.

How It Changes Floor 4: No access until clear.

### 9. Party Weaponizes Speech

Conditions: Party uses recorded speech to coerce, humiliate, or falsely bind a target.

Immediate Result: Clear may happen, but record is morally dangerous.

Reward: 15 NC, no Listening Mark.

Scar/Debt/Heat Impact: Heat or legal attention rises; Echo Attention follows to Nexus rumor.

Public Reaction: Some admire cleverness; vulnerable witnesses distrust them.

Faction Reaction: Ledger Court wary, CodeX intrigued, Last Light displeased.

Tower Reaction: Mark sounds sharp when spoken of.

Next-Session Opener: A harmed witness or echo appears in rumor.

How It Changes Floor 4: A speech weapon can rebound.

### 10. Party Protects Silence

Conditions: Party preserves Silent Gallery, Broken Silence Camp, or quiet truth at cost.

Immediate Result: Clear with protected silence record.

Reward: 20 NC, Silence Token, Hand-Signal Slate.

Scar/Debt/Heat Impact: Heat cools if silence prevented public harm.

Public Reaction: Less flashy but respected by careful runners.

Faction Reaction: Remnant Veil and Last Light notice.

Tower Reaction: Mark is nearly invisible until the PC listens.

Next-Session Opener: A quiet NPC asks for help outside the spotlight.

How It Changes Floor 4: A hidden route responds to silence.

# RETURN TO NEXUS AFTER ORIENTATION TRIAL 3

Read-Aloud:

> The training threshold releases you into the Forecourt, and for one impossible second the whole Nexus sounds too loud. Coins, boots, breath, jokes, vendors, bells, wings, wheels, paper, names. Your Trial 3 record writes itself above you in silver script, and everyone nearby lowers their voice without knowing why.

Public Record:

- `TEAM [NAME]: ORIENTATION TRIAL 3 CLEAR. METHOD: QUIET/LISTENING/LOUD/VOICE-COST/DEAL-TRUTH.`
- `NOISE RECORD: LOW/MODERATE/HIGH.`
- `RECORDED PHRASE: [DM selects one meaningful phrase from play].`
- `EXTRACTION: NONE/USED.`
- `VOICE STRAIN: NONE/NOTED.`

GUIDY Reaction: "I have created seven new warnings about talking. I am proud of only four."

Marik Reaction: Marik asks whether any recorded speech could create legal trouble, especially if the party corrected or weaponized a deal.

Aria Reaction: Aria wants to know the phrase the Tower recorded. She offers to turn it into a song, a warning, or a secret.

Felix Reaction: Felix asks whether silence tokens can be appraised, then admits he is uncomfortable pricing quiet.

CodeX Reaction: CodeX asks for audio residue and offers 15 NC or a portal-world rumor.

Rival Team Reaction: The Glass Comets challenge the public record if Trial 2 rival mark or Trial 3 loud clear made the party look faster, cleaner, or more disciplined than them.

Price Changes:

- Earplugs, chalk slates, and message tokens rise by 1-3 NC.
- Magical silence consultation costs 10 NC.
- Legal transcript copies cost 5 NC, free if Ledger Court reputation is strong.
- Reliable portal-world and Spire-preparation rumor prices rise by 5 NC if the party's record is dramatic.

Rumor Changes:

- "The third floor stole someone's voice."
- "They corrected a deal the Tower remembered."
- "Silence can be a treasure now."
- "Glass Comets say the record missed a shortcut."
- "Vane's people hate floors that remember exact words."

Faction Reaction:

- Wardens value controlled noise and clean records.
- Guild wants to monetize sound tokens.
- Spire Seekers celebrate loud clears.
- Salvage Union updates extraction advice for sound hazards.
- Ledger Court watches deal-truth results.
- Codebreakers want audio residue.
- Last Light supports voice recovery and protected silence.
- Remnant Veil studies quiet marks and echoed names.

Effect on Contract Hall/Vane Thread: If the party gains a corrected transcript or deal-truth clear, Vane's network becomes more cautious. If the party weaponizes speech, Vane's side may later accuse them of doing what they condemned. If shortcut debt remains, Guild brokers may fold it into old legal pressure.

Effect on Sel/Kessa: Sel is fascinated and frightened by a floor that records exact words. Kessa wants to know whether silence felt safe or like hiding. Either can help interpret a recorded phrase if treated with care.

If the Party Hides Their Result: Deception or Performance DC 14 hides one embarrassing tone, such as loud clear or voice strain, but not the public record. A success lets the party control the story for one day. A partial success creates a rumor gap. A failure lets a rival or sponsor define the story first.

## Post-Trial 3 Downtime

Rest: A long rest is available after return unless the party immediately chooses further trouble. Voice Strain clears after a long rest unless tied to a scar. A short rest clears mild throat pain but not public record.

Scar Treatment: Sound-related scars can be treated by Last Light care, Aria's vocal exercises, Ledger transcript correction, or quiet meditation. Typical cost is 5-10 NC or a small favor.

Route-Token Review: The party can identify route tokens with Arcana, Investigation, or History DC 13. Felix can appraise sale value. GUIDY can explain public record effects.

Identifying Boons: A boon can be identified during a short rest or by a service costing 5 NC. The player should know the mechanical effect before choosing to use it.

Training: A PC can spend downtime practicing hand signals, quiet movement, route marking, or legal phrasing. Grant advantage on one related check in the next portal-world session, orientation trial, or Spire-preparation scene if the scene is played or paid for with 5 NC.

Faction Messages: Choose two based on outcomes: sponsor demand, CodeX offer, Warden caution, Ledger request, Guild purchase offer, Last Light support, Spire challenge, Remnant omen.

Rumor Gathering: Persuasion, Investigation, or Insight DC 13 learns one rumor about portal worlds or later Spire preparation: stairs that trade memories, doors that demand proof of route, or a checkpoint that listens for team name.

Preparation for Next Canonical Play: Ask the party what they repair, what they buy, what route tokens they carry, who knows their recorded phrase, and which portal world or preparation path they choose next.

### Downtime Scene 1. Aria Asks What the Tower Recorded

Read-Aloud:

> Aria holds up one finger before anyone speaks. "Careful. After that listening trial, the first version matters."

NPC Goal: Aria wants the true emotional shape of the floor record.

Player Choice: Share the phrase, keep it private, ask her to bury it in song, ask her to amplify it.

Check/DC: Performance DC 13 shapes public song; Insight DC 13 sees Aria will protect a painful truth if trusted.

Reward: Public reputation tone chosen by party.

Consequence: False heroic framing may echo badly if exposed by rivals.

Hook to Next Expedition: Aria heard a verse about a staircase that "charges memory."

### Downtime Scene 2. GUIDY Creates a Silence Etiquette Card

Read-Aloud:

> GUIDY projects a tiny card: `POLITE SILENCE: NOT THE SAME AS PANIC, SECRECY, OR BEING DEAD.` It waits for praise.

NPC Goal: GUIDY wants to help with communication protocols.

Player Choice: Accept card, edit it, laugh, ask for tactical version.

Check/DC: Arcana or Insight DC 12 helps GUIDY tune the advice.

Reward: Once before the next major expedition ends, party can lower Echo/Noise-style pressure by 1 when following a clear communication plan.

Consequence: Ignoring it has no penalty, but GUIDY sulks for one scene.

Hook to Next Expedition: GUIDY notes the next route may respond to "what you spend."

### Downtime Scene 3. Marik Asks About Shortcut Debt

Read-Aloud:

> Marik taps the public record where a red-gold thread appears. "Tell me whether this is a problem or just Tower poetry."

NPC Goal: Marik wants to prevent shortcut debt from becoming civic debt.

Player Choice: Explain, ask for Warden advice, hide debt, transfer claim, challenge public record.

Check/DC: Persuasion DC 13 for help; Legal Cant DC 14 separates shortcut debt from legal debt; Deception DC 15 hides it for now.

Reward: Warden note that reduces one public shortcut-debt complication.

Consequence: Lying and later exposure increases heat.

Hook to Next Expedition: Marik warns that repeated training marks can become legal arguments outside.

### Downtime Scene 4. Felix Wants to Price Route Tokens

Read-Aloud:

> Felix places three velvet pads on his counter. "One for things worth money, one for things worth more than money, and one for things that get people killed because they confuse the first two."

NPC Goal: Felix wants market access to route tokens without angering the Tower or Wardens.

Player Choice: Sell, refuse, ask appraisal, trade for supplies, ask what buyers want.

Check/DC: Insight DC 13 sees Felix fears selling to reckless teams; Persuasion DC 14 improves trade; Investigation DC 13 learns token buyers.

Reward: 10-25 NC or discounted supplies.

Consequence: Selling a route token can create rival advantage.

Hook to Next Expedition: A buyer seeks tokens for a memory toll.

### Downtime Scene 5. CodeX Wants Audio Residue

Read-Aloud:

> Your cup vibrates. Black text ripples across the surface: `SELL ME THE SOUND THE TOWER KEPT.`

NPC Goal: CodeX wants recorded phrases, stolen voice residue, or Choir transcript fragments.

Player Choice: Sell, redact, refuse, trade for rumor, report CodeX.

Check/DC: Arcana DC 14 redacts identity; Persuasion DC 14 sets price; Insight DC 13 sees CodeX is tracking Executioner-adjacent records.

Reward: 15 NC or a portal-world clue.

Consequence: Warden suspicion if raw records move illegally.

Hook to Next Expedition: CodeX says, "The next paths spend what the first three trials recorded."

### Downtime Scene 6. Rival Team Challenges the Public Record

Read-Aloud:

> The Glass Comets' notice appears under yours: `CONTEXT MISSING. ROUTE CREDIT DISPUTED.`

NPC Goal: Rival team wants attention, credit, and leverage.

Player Choice: Ignore, answer publicly, request comparison hearing, challenge to future route, offer shared credit.

Check/DC: Performance DC 13 wins public tone; Persuasion DC 14 offers clean rivalry; Investigation DC 14 proves route claim.

Reward: Public reputation +1 or rival respect.

Consequence: Escalating insult makes rivals interfere near the next public expedition.

Hook to Next Expedition: Glass Comets announce they will beat the party to the next visible checkpoint.

## Chunk 04 Handouts

### Player Handout: Trial 2 Shortcut Warning Scratch

```
THE SHORT WAY WAS REAL.
THE COST WAS REAL.

WE WERE NOT CHEATED.
WE WERE IN A HURRY.
THAT WAS ENOUGH.
```

### Player Handout: Runner's Cache Note

```
Take what keeps you alive.
Leave what keeps the next team alive.

If you make a route safer, mark it.
If you make a route worse, own it.
If you save time, ask who paid.
```

### Player Handout: Thread Door Inscription

```
NAME WHAT SAVED TIME.
NAME WHO PAID.

A shortcut with a known cost is a choice.
A shortcut with a hidden cost is a chain.
A shortcut with no named owner is waiting to become one.
```

### Player Handout: Trial 3 Silence Etiquette Fragment

```
SILENCE IS NOT EMPTY.

In silence, write.
In darkness, signal.
When afraid, touch twice.
When separated, wait for the third pulse.
When a voice repeats you, listen before answering.
```

### Player Handout: Recorded Deal Transcript

```
RECORDED PHRASE:
"I accept the delivery."

MISSING CONTEXT:
The recipient was not shown the hidden obligation.
The witness bell did not ring cleanly.
The record contains pressure from an unnamed third party.

STATUS:
Truth incomplete. Consent contested. Mercy relevant.
```

### Player Handout: Quiet Checkpoint Veil Inscription

```
WHAT MUST BE SAID?
WHAT MUST BE HEARD?
WHAT MUST BE LEFT QUIET?

Speak one truth.
Hear one truth.
Protect one silence.
```

### Player Handout: Public Trial 3 Record

```
TOWER ASCENSION PUBLIC RECORD

TEAM: ______________________
FLOOR: 3
STATUS: ____________________
METHOD: ____________________
NOISE RECORD: ______________
RECORDED PHRASE: ___________
VOICE STRAIN: ______________
EXTRACTION USED: ___________
PUBLIC NOTE: _______________
```

## Chunk 04 Troubleshooting

Players Try to Speedrun Trial 2: Let them. Give clear movement checks, Time Saved, and visible toll signs. If they ignore signs, shortcut debt follows rather than stopping progress.

Players Refuse All Shortcuts: Patient routes work. Reward preparation, cache care, and route security. The public record may call them slow, but the Tower does not punish caution.

Players Try to Claim Ownership of a Route: Allow it if they mark cost, secure danger, or prove abandoned claim. A false claim creates rival/owner attention.

Players Attack Shortcut Owner: Pikkit defends, flees, or bargains. Killing or dispersing Pikkit does not erase route debt unless the party proves ownership was false or repairs the route.

Players Split Up: Warn through route marks and sound echoes. Run quick cuts and reunite at F2-9 or F3-7 unless the table wants split play. Increase objective pressure, not lethal ambushes.

Players Argue Loudly on Trial 3: Let echoes repeat useful and embarrassing phrases. Raise Noise or Echo Attention, then present a silent route or listening action to recover.

Players Try Magical Silence: It works. It reveals silent writing and blocks some sound hazards. It also prevents hearing warnings and can attract Hush Wraith if used to erase a pleading or true record.

Players Use Telepathy or Message: Let it support coordination. The floor records intent if the magic carries bargains, threats, lies, or oaths. Pure tactical coordination is clever play.

Players Weaponize Recorded Speech: Let it work in the moment if the record supports it, then attach moral and public consequences if they coerce, humiliate, or falsify.

Players Refuse to Speak at All: Trial 3 can be cleared through writing, signals, listening, and silence. The Choir still asks how they protect true records.

Players Want to Extract Mid-Trial: Use the extraction procedure from the training appendix. Trial 2 extraction records route state. Trial 3 extraction records noise and voice strain.

A PC Drops to 0 HP: Enemies do not execute downed PCs in these early floors unless the party has created extreme lethal circumstances. Use extraction, retreat, or ally protection.

A PC Dies: Apply the three lives rule. Public record notes the floor, method, and extraction state. Give space for downtime grief and consequence.

Players Want to Go Back to Nexus Between Every Room: They can retreat only through known exits and return thresholds. Leaving mid-floor usually resets some route state, raises public attention, or costs time. Do not trap them, but make repeated exits visible.

Players Want to Continue Straight to Real Spire Progression: Point them back to the Executioner warning. Additional safe training does not unlock true Spire floors. End this appendix after post-Trial 3 downtime or at the decision point, then return to portal-world preparation or a later dedicated Spire chapter.

## Training Chunk 04 Handoff Summary

Trial 2 Outcome: Record Patient Clear, Fast Honest Clear, Shortcut Debt Clear, Rival Mark Clear, Owner Bargain Clear, Collapse Survival, Extraction Used, Forced Retreat, Route Secured for Future, or Party Ignores the Rule.

Trial 3 Outcome: Record Quiet Clear, Loud Clear, Listening Clear, Voice-Cost Clear, Deal-Truth Clear, Shortcut Debt Echo, Extraction Used, Forced Retreat, Party Weaponizes Speech, or Party Protects Silence.

Party Level: Default remains level 2. If the party was level 1 and cleared Trial 2 or Trial 3, award level 2. If using faster advancement, Trial 3 clear can mark progress toward level 3 but should not replace portal-world leveling.

Lives Lost: Record remaining life counters and public death phrases.

Scars Gained: Record route scars, shortcut debt marks, voice strain, silence scars, or sound-related tells.

Boons Gained: Record Trial 2 boons, Trial 3 boons, limits, and expiration points.

Route Tokens Gained: Record Trial 2 threaded route token, shortcut mark, silence token, listening mark, voice pearl, and any carried Trial 1 token.

Shortcut Debt Status: None, paid, challenged, transferred, owner-bargained, rival-claimed, sponsor-held, or carried into the next expedition as a training complication.

Silence/Listening Mark Status: None, token held, listening mark active, voice pearl held, protected silence public, or weaponized speech concern.

Public Reputation: Record whether the party is known as careful, fast, debt-marked, owner-bargained, rival-contested, quiet, loud, truth-correcting, voice-cost, or dangerous with words.

Faction Reactions:

- Wardens: heat, public safety, and speech weaponization.
- Guild: route token prices, shortcut debt, and sponsor value.
- Spire Seekers: speed and public daring.
- Salvage Union: collapse survival and extraction records.
- Ledger Court: recorded deals and consent language.
- Codebreakers: shortcut marks and audio residue.
- Last Light: protected silence, voice recovery, and mercy.
- Remnant Veil: echoed voices and quiet marks.

Rival Team Reaction: Glass Comets may challenge, mock, respect, copy, or try to beat the party to the next visible checkpoint.

Unresolved Vane/Debt/Legal Hooks: Note whether Trial 3 corrected a deal, exposed a phrase, carried shortcut debt, or gave Vane's side grounds for accusation.

Clues Learned:

- Shortcuts are not free.
- Speed can become debt.
- Routes can be owned or claimed.
- Preparation makes risk honest.
- Chosen risk differs from tricked consent.
- The Tower records speech.
- Silence reveals routes.
- Listening is active.
- Communication is a resource.
- Witnessed deals and false consent echo in Tower law.

Next Canonical Setup Needs: Carry route debt, public record tone, rival pressure, voice marks, and any Trial 3 recorded phrase into portal-world systems, Nexus faction scenes, or later Spire preparation.

Later Spire Setup Needs: Carry route security and evidence of how the party handles speed, speech, and public cost when the campaign eventually returns to true Spire chapters.

Expected Next Repaired Chunk: The next canonical chunk should build portal-world systems, character slots, portal access, followers, item boundaries, and the first full portal-world campaign path. Do not continue to safe Spire Floors 4-5 from this appendix.
